Art World

International Art Exhibition 171

– Chen Deming

The French Salon exhibition and the British Royal Exhibition are both watched by the world. However, these exhibitions are limited to a narrow scope within one country. The one that brings together masterpieces of modern art from various countries in one place for a grand exhibition is the International Art Exhibition held in Venice, Italy. The Venice International Art Exhibition is a general exhibition of art from various countries in the world, just as the Summer Olympics is a general competition of sports from various countries. The exhibition is held every two years in the city of Venice, Italy, because Italy is the source of art in the world, and Venice is the art center of Italy, and the scenery is beautiful and picturesque, making it most suitable for holding art exhibitions. Because this exhibition is held every two years and the venue is in Venice, it is named the Venice Biennale (VeniceBiennialExhilition). Every time the exhibition is held, not to mention that the whole city of Venice is empty and people go to visit, people from other parts of Italy and art lovers from Europe and the United States also go to visit from thousands of miles away. It is truly the most grand event in international art. This year's 17th exhibition was held in the summer, and the grand occasion was no less than in the past. European and American countries and Japan in East Asia all had works on display (our country is the only one without any products, and I don't know what the Chinese people think about this). The countries with the most products, such as Italy, France, Germany, England, the United States, the Netherlands, Belgium, Hungary, and Czechoslovakia, all opened up a separate venue for display and exhibition. The grand occasion of the exhibition will be described separately as follows:

Italian Department

Italy is the host of the International Exhibition, so let's first talk about the Italian Department in the exhibition. Because Italy is the host of the conference, there are so many products that it is dazzling, making people feel like they are on Shanyin Road, with too many things to see. However, these thousands of works have a unified color, which is the color of restoration (I use the word restoration instead of restoration because they are not returning to classicism, but abandoning futurism, etc.). Now let's talk about painting and sculpture separately.

Painting

Italian paintings in this exhibition can be divided into three categories based on the subject matter:

(A) Historical Paintings

The revival of Italian historical paintings is a natural result, because in recent years, the activities of Mussolini and his Fascist Party are excellent ready-made subjects for painters, which they cannot abandon. Therefore, modern Italian historical paintings are different from historical paintings that usually depict events and figures from the past. In fact, they are realistic paintings of Italian political activities. We call them historical paintings for the sake of future generations. These paintings are full of modern meaning, unlike historical paintings that depict ancient people and ancient objects, which cannot arouse the interest of modern people. At the same time, these paintings are not political propaganda like Soviet Russian art, but purely narrative paintings. Among the historical painters, ArnaldoCarpananettl, PrimsConti, and TononaspCascella are the most worthy of mention. They faithfully reproduce the past activities and revolutionary process of the Fascist Party on the screen. Their paintings can be compared to the great paintings of Delacroix, the great French romantic painter of the nineteenth century. The Marseillaise aroused extraordinary excitement in the audience.

(B) Figure Paintings

Italy has always been famous for its figure paintings. There are many noteworthy works in this International Exhibition. These works are noteworthy for two reasons: one is because the figures in the paintings are noteworthy, such as the portraits of celebrities such as poets D'Annunzio and Novaro made by Bucci, DeMaria, Galanti, Frescia, Lambertini, and Casella. The other is known for its technique, such as the realistic figure paintings of GiussppeAmlsani, Saliett, Monti, Gaudenzii, and Conti Bucci, and the poetic figure paintings of Vonni Vagnetti Bucci, all of which have deeply understood the essence of art in the Renaissance era, and Feltrinelli's color-based figure paintings are especially eye-catching.

(C) Landscape Paintings

Italian landscape paintings, whether in terms of theme or style, are full of local scenery. Bacci, Caligiani, Dani, Gueriu, and Monti depicted the Tuscan landscape. Tosi, Pratell, Arata, Fuimi, and Prada depicted the Lombardy landscape. Figiari and Biasi depicted island scenery. The landscape painters influenced by France are Sobrero, Chessa, and Paolucci.

Sculpture

Recent Italian sculpture art, as seen from this international development, has resolutely returned to the path of classicism. It goes without saying that old writers such as Andereorti, Maraini, Romanelli, Secretary General of the Congress, and Baroni all studied ancient sculpture as the basis for their creation. For example, FrancescoMessina extracted the essence and hints of the sculptures of Pompeii (which was submerged by volcanic eruptions centuries ago and has recently been excavated, yielding many ancient artworks) to create their analytical sculptures. Marchini found the secret of rhyme in the sculptures of the Roman Empire era. Marini obtained his extraordinary realistic ability from ancient Etruscan sculptures. Some sculptors take modern athletes and athletes as objects to express strong physiques, just like ancient Greek sculptors used warriors and athletes as themes. Among the female sculptors who can be mentioned are EglePozzi and MaryalLednicka, both of whom are young female writers with artistic beauty.

In addition, black and white paintings (including sketches, prints, woodcuts, etc.) are also very noteworthy. The representative writers are Bartoli, Carbonati, Mazzonizarini, Disertori, Magnavacca, Mauroner, and Bucci, all of whom are internationally renowned writers. Their tastes and styles are all modern, among which Bartolini and Bucci are the most outstanding.

The most memorable thing in the Italian Department is actually a room of works by the painter Modigliani. Modigliani was a genius in the modern art world, but his encounter was extremely pitiful. Because of his political party relationship, he was not tolerated by the government. He lived in Paris, France, and engaged in painting. His paintings were too high in style and were not recognized by the people of the time. No one bought them. In 1920, he starved to death in a slum in Paris. Only in recent years have his paintings been valued. Now he has occupied a permanent place in the history of art. This time, the International Development brought together more than 50 of his paintings made in his life and exhibited them in a room, which was unprecedented. There were many viewers in this room, all of whom lingered and were reluctant to leave. One reason was to appreciate Modigliani's superb art, and the other was to lament his tragic life.

French Department

France is the center of modern art and naturally occupies a leading position in the International Art Exhibition. There are too many French artists, and they are all well-known, so I will not describe them in detail here. However, we can summarize by saying that French art in this exhibition shows the French national character more significantly than in the past. The most eye-catching painter is VanDongen. He is the pride of the modern French art world. He uses rich and gorgeous colors to depict beautiful women and concubines inside and outside Paris, which are full of fascination. The International Exhibition specially opened a room to display his paintings, which has a strong attraction to the audience.

German Department

The German paintings displayed in this International Art Exhibition can also be summarized in one sentence, that is, the German national character they show is also more significant than in the past. German art is inherently rich in national character. In the years after the end of the European War, the German art world once joined hands with the art worlds of other European countries, but now they have parted ways and taken their own paths. In the International Exhibition, MaxBeckmann's comprehensive paintings, OttoDix's integrated figure paintings, and Barlack's strong and expressive sculptures all show the strong German national character, which is in stark contrast to VanDongen's gorgeous paintings and Despian's soft sculptures in the French Department.

British Department

The United Kingdom, which is famous for its conservatism, is the only one in this international art exhibition that tends to restoration to advocate for new art. For example, PaulNash in painting is the only surviving representative of Futurism in this international exhibition. In the previous International Exhibition, Futurist works filled all the rooms. For example, RichardSickert is an Impressionist painter, and GlynPhilpot's decorative paintings are full of modern mystery. In terms of sculpture, Moore's works are between black art and Cubism. JohnSkeaping's sculptures contain primitivity. In addition, John Nash, such as the watercolor paintings of the Paul Nash brothers, Dodd, the engraving of John, and the prints of Sickert and Rusbbwry are the best in the audience.

American Department

The United States has a separate department in the International Art Exhibition, which is a notable event that began this year. With an independent department, people have a whole understanding of American art. Previously, people thought that the United States was a country without art because they did not have a deep understanding of American art. However, from this International Art Exhibition, it seems that the United States is indeed a rising star, and the future is very bright. In this exhibition, the paintings that are worthy of mention are the portrait paintings of GeorzeBrush, AlexanderBrook, JSidneyDickinson, NicholaiTechin, and CharlesHopkins. The figure paintings of GeorgeBellows, CeciliaBeaux, MauriceFromkes, and KarlAnderson are especially outstanding and have the style of masters. The new writers are HoratisWalker and Katz. The sculptures that are worthy of mention are MalvinaHoffmann and MccartanEward.

The above-mentioned countries are the most important and most noticed in the International Art Exhibition. As for other countries, or only a small department is set up, or the exhibitions are combined, which are relatively secondary and will not be mentioned in detail.

In summary, the International Art Exhibition is a general expression of the artistic activities of various nations in the world. We have seen the following key points regarding the recent trends in world art in this International Exhibition:

Pay attention to the expression of national character

On the History of Modern Art Trends 172

– Yi Kang

An Art History Dominated by National Color

The development of European art trends from the French Revolution to the past hundred years is an extremely complex and rapid page in the history of art. During this era, because of the liberation of political thought and the enlightenment of politics, almost all the people in Europe ran out of the shackles of the old days and participated in the creation of art. Therefore, the strong colors of each nation's territory and the spirit of the storm era are presented in the art of the entire Europe. Therefore, we must trace the modern art to this great period, and especially important is not to ignore that the main trend of art in this period is the national color.

In the world's history of art trends literature, Professor Takaho Itagaki's "History of Modern Art Trends" is worth mentioning, which uses national color as the center to describe it. He abandoned the scattered and non-central thinking narratives of those who have studied art history in the past and made a bold attempt based on a fundamental concept and principle. Therefore, it is a unique success for him to describe the history of modern art trends with national color, because art, like literature, cannot reconcile exoticism or suppress local colors. Therefore, the depiction of art in Northern Europe, such as Sweden and Norway, depicts everything in the ice and snow and half-year daylight. French, German, and Italian art has the rich colors of Southern Europe. Slavic art has the vast continent's melancholy and fortitude. Indian and black art has strong national colors. Therefore, in his book, he uses the scale of national color to measure the art trends of various nations in this era. In this way, in his scale, we can see the qualities and significance of the art produced in that era.

In the history of art, the recently popular artistic will (Kurstwollen) does not have any consistent and unified concept to indicate the content. Therefore, some people think that this sentence refers to the form of creation of an era divided according to cultural history, and some scholars use it as the meaning of the expression style inherent in a nation. However, the scale for evaluating art cannot be immutable, just as relativity replaces absolutism in physics, the examination of art also raises doubts in an immutable scale evaluation. Therefore, people who use and admire artistic will abandon its permanent value in doubt and seek another relative scale to estimate the value of the art of each era and each nation with the scale of that era and that nation. This new method has aroused people's attention, and the horizons of art historians have become broader and the understanding has clearly progressed. In this way, the artist will not be biased towards one aspect, that is, the early foreigners, but in this method, a new art historian should be a fair observer, and at the same time, should try to be a warm sympathizer, and even more should try to be a sharp insight, and a new cliché gradually emerged in the new method.

Therefore, the leader who insists on the position of shaping and firmly defends the territory, the French nation, who has dominated the European art world since the eighteenth century and has become the keynote of the art trend, has continued to grasp the long-term rule, and the one who is opposed to France is the Germans among the Northern European nations. The French are always true realists in terms of shaping, focusing on practical work, while the Northern European nations, although strong in character, are ultimately biased towards idealism, faithful to their own beliefs. Therefore, they do not use models and think about the mysteries of the non-human world. Therefore, they have always formed a decisive different direction from the painting school in Southern Europe.

The whole book takes national color as the warp and the thought of the times as the weft. In the nine chapters, it tells about the history of art trends after the French Revolution. He is the first person in the writing world to use national color as the center to study art trends. The Japanese version is published by Daiyoroi Kaku in Tokyo, and the Beixin Bookstore in China has a translation of Lu Xun before it changed direction. It is worth reading this masterpiece that organizes the history of art trends with a new method.

Art World Manuscript Regulations 173

(1) The text is limited to news, reviews, and introductions of recent art (painting, music, sculpture, architecture, drama, etc.) and literature at home and abroad.

(3) Photos are limited to recent portraits of domestic and foreign writers and their works, and various photographs related to the text.

Social News

An Interview with George Bernard Shaw (3) 174

— Lin

Meeting Isadora Duncan

My encounter with Isadora… I've never seen her dance, which is a rare thing," Shaw said. "At that time, I did something I don't often do: I went into society. I attended a tea party hosted by Lady Scott.

I remember sitting on the sofa when suddenly, a woman I didn't know sat down beside me and asked,

'Are you Shaw?' 'Yes,' I replied.

She stretched out her arms. 'Come to me,' this woman said, 'I will love you forever!'

Shaw laughed as he recounted this story, as if the memory made him very happy.

I asked, "And what did you do?"

"I performed the second act of Tristan and Isolde," Shaw said. "For about an hour, Isadora and I continued talking. I don't remember what we said to each other, but I knew the bystanders were delighted to listen to our every word. I think at first, my hostess must have been a little anxious about how I would handle the situation."

I said, "I can well imagine the scene. Isadora often told me she should marry you or Augustus John. What was your impression of her?"

"Oh," Shaw said quietly, "The strange thing is, I don't remember much at all. The photos taken of her have some resemblance. Her photos are rare because each one seems to capture her unique style. To me, she seemed very plump. Oh, and she was very much like a piece of candy that has been struck."

I said to Shaw, "Poor Isadora, he described her perfectly. When he met her, she was already indifferent to her appearance, especially after the tragedy occurred, her demeanor suffered many reactions."

"She has the cheeks of a devil," Shaw said. "She speaks her mind freely. Yet, her skill lies in preventing others from calling her a demon."

At this moment, Shaw was sitting directly across from me, his attitude very amiable. I thought this was an opportunity to resolve a widely circulated anecdote about the playwright and Isadora.

According to this anecdote, there was a time when Isadora's beauty was considered by sculptors and artists to be the most beautiful in the world. She wrote a letter to Shaw, asking if he would be willing to have a child with her. She seemed to have said, "You have the most brilliant mind in the world, and I have the most beautiful body. So let us produce a perfect child." To this request, Shaw replied, "But what if the child is born with my body and your mind?"

This anecdote made Shaw laugh. All great writers find their own witticisms amusing.

"Actually," Shaw said, "this wasn't Isadora who proposed this to me. There are many famous women involved in the stories about me, especially Isadora Duncan. In fact, I received this strange proposition from a foreign actress whose name you wouldn't know, and I've forgotten it myself. But I definitely had that response."

Without the slightest conceit

One can say things to Shaw that one cannot say to ordinary people, because this famous playwright has much to be conceited about, but he has no conceit at all. So, I asked him a question that very few writers of his stature would be willing to answer. I suspect very few young people of my standing would be willing to ask him. But it is my belief that the more intelligent a person is, the less resentment they have toward a small, frank inquiry. In this particular situation, I gratefully say that my belief was fully proven.

"Tell me, Mr. Shaw," I said, "What's wrong with George Moore? He recently said he thought you were so vulgar. He also criticized you for publicizing unimportant things like your change of address. And he said you love talking about yourself so much that your plays give him a headache."

I know there are some celebrities who, if told for the first time about others' criticism of them, would blush and get angry without a doubt. But Shaw just smiled and said in a calm, graceful tone,

"I don't see anything wrong with George's jokes. I suspect that if he thinks I'm excessively vulgar, it's because a person without vulgarity is like someone without a stomach; they cannot survive. I publicized my change of address to teach George not to send the wrong letters. He can't blame me too much. I talk about myself because I have many meaningful and interesting experiences that can serve as useful evidence. I should do more of this work, but I feel a little tired and want to avoid social responsibilities. As for anyone whose plays sometimes give some people a headache, if George can't resist reading them, he can put them away. His discomfort might be good for him." (The End)

New Eurasia Air Route to Begin Next Spring 176

Prepared by Russia

Vladivostok Report: The air route connecting Europe and the East, between Berlin, Moscow, and Vladivostok, is scheduled to begin next spring. The entire line will be prepared solely by Russia without external assistance. Three years have already been completed. In the future, the Moscow airship field will become a major international air hub.

Agricultural Production in the Eastern Provinces Expected to Increase 177

Approximately 100,000 Tons

Dalian Report: According to the South Manchuria Railway Survey Department's second harvest forecast for agricultural products in the Eastern Provinces this year (August 24), the total is estimated to be approximately 18,380,000 tons, an increase of 100,000 tons compared to last year. The contents of important grains are as follows: Soybeans and other beans: 5,400,000 tons; Sorghum: 4,680,000 tons; Millet: 3,280,000 tons; Corn: 580,000 tons; Wheat: 1,390,000 tons; Rice: 300,000 tons.

United States Cracks Down on Fake Antique Imports 178

Those Caught Will Be Fined 25% of the Original Price

After the United States implemented new tariffs, the import tax rates on industrial products were increased, while the import tax rates on artworks and antiques were reduced. As a result, antique rugs and other items that had been absent from the United States for many years were imported in large numbers. However, the U.S. tax authorities, aware that many fakes are mixed in with artworks, have specifically stipulated that those caught will be fined 25% of the original price. The U.S. Ambassador in Paris has issued a public notice, which has caused anxiety among merchants in this sector. According to a well-known antique dealer in Paris, this law will mean that those importing fakes will sometimes pay total taxes reaching 90% of the original value, which is a waste compared to importing genuine goods.

Last Year's Production Value in Taiwan 179

Total production value approximately 63,300,000 packages, an increase of 8,800,000 yuan compared to five years ago.

Taipei Report: The survey of Taiwan's production value last year has now been completed. The agricultural production value is estimated at 31,171,100 yuan, the aquatic production value at 20,000,000 yuan, the mineral production value at 16,000,000 yuan, and the total production value, including un-surveyed industrial and forestry production values, is approximately 63,370,000 yuan, an increase of 8,800,000 yuan compared to the previous highest record of 62,498,000 yuan in 1915. Taking the index of 29 years ago as 100, it increased to 747 in 1914 and 870 the year before last.

Alarm Clock Used as a Gun 180

Threw It at Burglar's Head; Police Arrived After Hearing the Sound; Burglar Was Knocked Unconscious

Fayetteville, North Carolina Report: A long-term prisoner named William Daley recently conspired with two accomplices to steal a car and was pursued. The other two escaped, while Daley fled into the backyard of a residence to hide. He accidentally touched a door lock, making a sound that woke the resident, a Mr. Davenport Newgent. Newgent, seeing that the only weapon at hand was an alarm clock, threw it from the window, hitting Daley on the head. The loud ringing attracted the police, who arrived to find Daley half-conscious from the blow.

Germany Proposes Regular German-Japanese Air Service 181

Japanese Authorities Express Agreement

Tokyo Report: Germany has proposed starting a regular air service between Europe and Asia to implement mail flights, publishing a major plan adapted to the era of practical aircraft. Germany will first conclude a friendly aviation treaty with China to realize a large-scale Sino-German joint venture airline. It is also planning to open an air route to Japan via Eastern Europe, Arabia, Indochina, and Vietnam. In late July, it submitted to the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Communications a request for an intercontinental regular airmail service, seeking Japan's overall attitude and approval. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs immediately held secret consultations with the Ministry of Communications and the Navy authorities. The consensus was that Japan currently has a regular air service plan between Fukuoka and Shanghai, which could be extended from Shanghai if the conditions are appropriate. Therefore, Japan replied to Germany, expressing support for the plan and requesting a specific proposal. The Japanese Ministry of Communications will proceed with specific plans after receiving the reply.

International Road Conference to Be Held Next Month 182

Discussing Road Paving and Other Matters

Washington Report: The Sixth International Road Conference is scheduled to be held in Washington from October 6. The agenda includes: 1. Road paving; 2. Unpaved rural roads; 3. Road policy and finance.

Sino-Japanese Trade Volume in August 183

Trade Deficit of 18,498,000 Yuan

According to the Japanese Ministry of Finance, in August, exports to China were 28,409,000 yuan, and imports were 9,911,000 yuan, resulting in a trade deficit of 18,498,000 yuan. Compared to August of last year, exports decreased by 18,834,000 yuan, and imports decreased by 5,471,000 yuan. The cumulative deficit since January is 49,514,000 yuan, a decrease of 53,666,000 yuan compared to last year's 103,180,000 yuan. In terms of regional comparison, only exports from South China (182,000 yuan) increased. Exports from the Eastern Provinces (2,541,000 yuan), North China (924,000 yuan), Central China (12,595,000 yuan), Dalian (1,780,000 yuan), and Hong Kong (896,000 yuan) all decreased. Similarly, only imports from Hong Kong (34,000 yuan) increased, while imports from the Eastern Provinces (865,000 yuan), North China (253,000 yuan), Central China (2,530,000 yuan), South China (303,000 yuan), and Dalian (1,529,000 yuan) all decreased.

(1) The text should be limited to news about domestic and foreign science, industry, commerce, agriculture, hygiene, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life.

(2) Drawings should be limited to lyrical paintings related to various aspects of social life.

(3) Photographs should be qualified for seasonal landscapes, animals and plants, people, and new photography. Photographs of seasonal landscapes featuring ladies are especially welcome.
